< review>
The KFC on E Hammer Ln is both delicious and easy to work with. I say that because my Grandma wanted KFC for her 90th birthday and they worked with us by accepting the order and payment over the phone. Additionally,  we were given the job of picking the food up. However, as usual, I was running late and was stressing that the food would be cold. I called the manager and he was so cool about it! I let him know I'd be coming from Galt and running late. He told me to call him when we got on the 99 and he would then cook and package it up for me whenever I was ready - and it was 5pm on a Saturday.  True to his word,  as soon as I got there the food was ready, I just had to sign the receipt and go. The food was delicious and hot, which made not just Grandma, but everyone happy!< /review>
